{"nick":"myndzi","message":"How does it work?","date":"2016-12-29T22:22:04.941Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"myndzi","message":"Nock works by overriding Node's http.request function. Also, it overrides http.ClientRequest too to cover for modules that use it directly.","date":"2016-12-29T22:22:05.107Z","type":"message"}
